Source Code

These source-code files were from the printout at the MIT Museum, with many thanks to Deborah Douglas, the Museum's Curator of Science and Technology, for releasing it to us. The printout was digitally photographed by Paul Fjeld. A team of volunteers transcribed the source code manually from these images or, where appropriate, modified already-transcribed but similar source Luminary 131 (Apollo 13) source code to agree with the images from the printout. Note that the page images presented online are of reduced quality, and that higher-quality images are available. Report any conversion errors or legibility problems in page images to info@sandroid.org. Notations on the program listing read, in part:

	GAP:  ASSEMBLE REVISION 001 OF AGC PROGRAM LMY99 BY NASA 2021112-061
	20'35 OCT. 28,1968
Note that the date is the date of the printout, not the date of the program revision.

Note: Notations below resembling this note are 21st-century annotations added by the Virtual AGC project, and are not original AGC source code. Page 390 

016452,000034:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME -- KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
016453,000035:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO -- 4           DATE -- 27 APRIL 1967           ASSEMBLY -- PINDANCE REV 18
016454,000036:                                                                                                  #  MOD BY -- FILENE
016455,000037:                                                                                                  #  LOG SECTION -- PINBALL GAME BUTTONS AND LIGHTS
016456,000038: 
016457,000039:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
016458,000040: 
016459,000041:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM PROGRAM OPERATES UNDER EXECUTIVE
016460,000042:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL AND PROCESSES INFORMATION EXCHANGED BETWEEN THE AGC AND THE
016461,000043:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTER OPERATOR.  THE INPUTS TO THE PROGRAM ARE FROM THE KEYBOARD,
016462,000044:                                                                                                  #  FROM INTERNAL PROGRAM, AND FROM THE UPLINK.
016463,000045: 
016464,000046:                                                                                                  #  THE LANGUAGE OF COMMUNICATION WITH THE PROGRAM IS A PAIR OF WORDS
016465,000047:                                                                                                  #  KNOWN AS VERB AND NOUN.  EACH OF THESE IS REPRESENTED BY A 2 CHARACTER
016466,000048:                                                                                                  #  DECIMAL NUMBER.  THE VERB CODE INDICATES WHAT ACTION IS TO BE TAKEN, THE
016467,000049:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE INDICATES TO WHAT THIS ACTION IS APPLIED.  NOUNS USUALLY
016468,000050:                                                                                                  #  REFER TO A GROUP OF ERASABLE REGISTERS.
016469,000051: 
016470,000052:                                                                                                  #  VERBS ARE GROUPED INTO DISPLAYS, LOADS, MONITORS (DISPLAYS THAT ARE
016471,000053:                                                                                                  #  UPDATED ONCE PER SECOND), SPECIAL FUNCTIONS, AND EXTENDED VERBS (THESE
016472,000054:                                                                                                  #  ARE OUTSIDE OF THE DOMAIN OF PINBALL AND CAN BE FOUND UNDER LOG SECTION
016473,000055:                                                                                                  #  'EXTENDED VERBS').
016474,000056: 
016475,000057:                                                                                                  #  A LIST OF VERBS AND NOUNS IS GIVEN IN LOG SECTION 'ASSEMBLY AND 
016476,000058:                                                                                                  #  OPERATION INFORMATION'.
016477,000059:

Ramón Alonso, one of the original AGC developers, provides a little more insight: Apparently, nobody had yet arrived at any kind of software requirements for the AGC's user interface when the desire arose within the Instrumentation Laboratory to set up a demo guidance-computer unit with which to impress visitors to the lab. Of course, this demo would have to do something, if it was going to be at all impressive, and to do something it would need some software. In short order, some of the coders threw together a demo program, inventing and using the verb/noun user-interface concept (in the whimsical fashion seen in much of this code), but without any idea that the verb/noun concept would somehow survive into the flight software. As time passed, and more and more people became familiar with the demo, nobody got around to inventing an improvement for the user interface, so the coders simply built it into the flight software without any specific requirements to do so.

However, that does not mean that the verb/noun interface was universally beloved. Ramón says that many objections were received from naysayers, such as "it's not scientific", "it's not dignified", or even "astronauts won't understand it". Even though the coders of the demo hadn't seriously intended the verb/noun interface to be used in any permanent way, it became a kind of devilish game to counter these objections with (perhaps) sophistic arguments as to why the interface was really a good one. In the end, the coders won. I don't know whether they were elated or dismayed by this victory.

The astronauts, of course, could understand the interface, but they did not like it. Most of them really wanted an interface much more like that they had used in aircraft: i.e., lots of dials and switches. Dave Scott is the the only astronaut I'm aware of who had kind words for it (or for the AGC in general), though we are told that Jim McDivitt wasn't necessary completely hostile to it.

—Ron Burkey, 07/2009

016512,000094: 
016513,000095:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCES --
016514,000096: 
016515,000097:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD:
016516,000098:                                                                                                  #  EACH DEPRESSION OF A KEYBOARD BUTTON ACTIVATES AN INTERRUPT KEYRUPT1
016517,000099:                                                                                                  #  AND PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO CHANNEL 15.  KEYRUPT1 PLACES THE KEY
016518,000100:                                                                                                  #  CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY
016519,000101:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM (AT 'CHARIN'), AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
016520,000102: 
016521,000103:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK:
016522,000104:                                                                                                  #  EACH WORD RECEIVED BY THE UPLINK ACTIVATES INTERRUPT UPRUPT, WHICH
016523,000105:                                                                                                  #  PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE
016524,000106:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM (AT 'CHARIN') AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
016525,000107: 
016526,000108:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS:
016527,000109:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS CALL PINBALL AT `NVSUB' WITH THE DESIRED VERB/NOUN
016528,000110:                                                                                                  #  CODE IN A (LOW 7 BITS FOR NOUN, NEXT 7 BITS FOR VERB).  DETAILS
016529,000111:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBED ON REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE 'NVSUB' AND 'NVSBWAIT' (SEE
016530,000112:                                                                                                  #  SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
016531,000113: 
016532,000114:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES --
016533,000115: 
016534,000116:                                                                                                  #        IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY EXTERNAL ACTION, THERE ARE FOUR EXITS:
016535,000117:                                                                                                  #                1)      ALL BUT (2), (3), AND (4) EXIT DIRECTLY TO ENDOFJOB.
016536,000118:                                                                                                  #                2)      EXTENDED VERBS GO TO THE EXTENDED VERB FAN AS PART OF THE

Page 391 

016538,000120:                                                                                                  #                        PINBALL EXECUTIVE JOB WITH PRIORITY 30000.  IT IS THE 
016539,000121:                                                                                                  #                        RESPONSIBILITY OF THE EXTEDED VERB CALLED TO EVENTUALLY
016540,000122:                                                                                                  #                        CHANGE PRIORITY (IF NECESSARY) AND DO AN ENDOFJOB.
016541,000123:                                                                                                  #                        ALSO PINBALL IS A NOVAC JOB.  EBANK SET FOR COMMON.
016542,000124:                                                                                                  #                3)      VERB 37.  CHANGE OF PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) CALLS 'V37' IN THE
016543,000125:                                                                                                  #                        SERVICE ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO
016544,000126:                                                                                                  #                        30000.  THE NEW PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IS LEFT IN A.
016545,000127:                                                                                                  #                4)      KEY RELEASE BUTTON CALLS 'PINBRNCH' IN THE DISPLAY INTERFACE
016546,000128:                                                                                                  #                        ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO 30000 IF 
016547,000129:                                                                                                  #                        THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IS OFF AND 'CADRSTOR' IS NOT +0.
016548,000130: 
016549,000131:                                                                                                  #  IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY INTERNAL PROGRAMS, EXIT FROM PINBALL IS BACK
016550,000132:                                                                                                  #  TO CALLING ROUTINE.  DETAILS DESCRIBED IN REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE
016551,000133:                                                                                                  #  'NVSUB' AND 'NVSBWAIT' (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
016552,000134: 
016553,000135:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES --
016554,000136: 
016555,000137:                                                                                                  #        EXTERNAL INITIATION:
016556,000138:                                                                                                  #        IF SOME IMPROPER SEQUENCE OF KEY CODES IS DETECTED, THE OPERATOR
016557,000139:                                                                                                  #        ERROR LIGHT IS TURNED ON AND EXIT IS TO 'ENDOFJOB'.
016558,000140: 
016559,000141:                                                                                                  #        INTERNAL PROGRAM INITIATION:
016560,000142:                                                                                                  #        IF AN ILLEGAL V/N COMBINATION IS ATTEMPTED, AN ABORT IS CAUSED
016561,000143:                                                                                                  #        (WITH OCTAL 01501).
016562,000144:                                                                                                  #        IF A SECOND ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL, AN ABORT IS
016563,000145:                                                                                                  #        CAUSED (WITH OCTAL 01206). THERE ARE TWO WAYS TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL:
016564,000146:                                                                                                  #                1) ENDIDLE OR DATAWAIT.
016565,000147:                                                                                                  #                2) NVSBWAIT, PRENVBSY, OR NVSUBUSY.
016566,000148: 
016567,000149:                                                                                                  #  CONDITIONS LEADING TO THE ABOVE ARE DESCRIBED IN FORTHCOMING MIT/IL
016568,000150:                                                                                                  #  E-REPORT DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
016569,000151: 
016570,000152:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT --
016571,000153: 
016572,000154:                                                                                                  #  INFORMATION TO BE SENT TO THE DISPLAY PANEL IS LEFT IN THE 'DSPTAB'
016573,000155:                                                                                                  #  BUFFERS REGISTERS (UNDER EXEC CONTROL). 'DSPOUT' (A PART OF T4RUPT)
016574,000156:                                                                                                  #  HANDLES THE PLACING OF THE 'DSPTAB' INFORMATION INTO OUTPUT CHANNEL 10
016575,000157:                                                                                                  #  IN INTERRUPT.
016576,000158: 
016577,000159:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION --
016578,000160: 
016579,000161:                                                                                                  #  FRESH START AND RESTART INITIALIZE THE NECESSARY E REGISTERS FOR
016580,000162:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IN 'STARTSUB'.  REGISTERS ARE:  DSPTAB BUFFER, CADRSTOR,
016581,000163:                                                                                                  #  REQRET, CLPASS, DSPLOCK, MONSAVE, MONSAVE1, VERBREG, NOUNREG, DSPLIST,
016582,000164:                                                                                                  #  DSPCOUNT, NOUT.
016583,000165: 
016584,000166:                                                                                                  #  A COMPLETE LIST OF ALL THE ERASABLES (BOTH RESERVED AND TEMPORARIES) FOR

Page 392 

016586,000168:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IS GIVEN BELOW.
016587,000169: 
016588,000170:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ARE OF GENERAL INTEREST --
016589,000171: 
016590,000172:                                                                                                  #  REMARKS CARDS PRECEDE THE REFERENCED SYMBOL DEFINITION.  SEE SYMBOL
016591,000173:                                                                                                  #  TABLE TO FIND APPROPRIATE PACE NUMBERS.
016592,000174: 
016593,000175:                                                                                                  #        NVSUB           CALLING POINT FOR INTERNAL USE OF PINBALL.
016594,000176:                                                                                                  #                        OF RELATED INTEREST     NVSBWAIT
016595,000177:                                                                                                  #                                                NVSUBUSY
016596,000178:                                                                                                  #                                                PRENVBSY
016597,000179: 
016598,000180:                                                                                                  #        ENDIDLE         ROUTINE FOR INTERNAL PROGRAMS WISHING TO TO SLEEP WHILE
016599,000181:                                                                                                  #                        AWAITING OPERATORS RESPONSE.
016600,000182: 
016601,000183:                                                                                                  #        DSPMM           ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY DISPLAY A DECIMAL
016602,000184:                                                                                                  #                        PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IN THE PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) LIGHTS.
016603,000185:                                                                                                  #                        (DSPMM DOES NOT DISPLAY DIRECTLY BUT ENTERS EXEC REQUEST
016604,000186:                                                                                                  #                        FOR DSPMMJB WITH PRIO 30000 AND RETURNS TO CALLER.)
016605,000187: 
016606,000188:                                                                                                  #        BLANKSUB        ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY BLANK ANY
016607,000189:                                                                                                  #                        COMBINATION OF THE DISPLAY REGISTERS R1, R2, R3.
016608,000190: 
016609,000191:                                                                                                  #        JAMTERM         ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY PERFORM THE
016610,000192:                                                                                                  #        JAMPROC         TERMINATE (V 34) OR PROCEED (V 33) FUNCTION.
016611,000193: 
016612,000194:                                                                                                  #        MONITOR         VERBS FOR PERIODIC (1 PER SEC) DISPLAY.
016613,000195: 
016614,000196:                                                                                                  #        PLEASE PERFORM, PLEASE MARK SITUATIONS
016615,000197:                                                                                                  #                REMARKS DESCRIBING HOW AN INTERNAL ROUTINE SHOULD HANDLE
016616,000198:                                                                                                  #                THESE SITUATIONS CAN BE FOUND JUST BEFORE 'NVSUB' (SEE
016617,000199:                                                                                                  #                SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
016618,000200: 
016619,000201:                                                                                                  #        THE NOUN TABLE FORMAT IS DESCRIBED ON A PAGE OF REMARKS CARDS JUST
016620,000202:                                                                                                  #        BEFORE 'DSPABC' (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
016621,000203: 
016622,000204:                                                                                                  #        THE NOUN TABLES THEMSELVES ARE FOUND IN LOG SECTION 'PINBALL NOUN
016623,000205:                                                                                                  #        TABLES'.
016624,000206: 
016625,000207:                                                                                                  #  FOR FURTHER DETAILS ABOUT OPERATION OF THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM
016626,000208:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM, SEE THE MISSION PLAN AND/OR MIT/IL E-2129
016627,000209:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
016628,000210:

The document described above, "Keyboard and Display Program Operation" by Alan I. Green and Robert J. Filene is available online at the Virtual AGC website. —Ron Burkey, 07/2009

016645,000227: 
016646,000228:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ASSIGNMENTS FOR PINBALL ARE MADE ELSEWHERE
016647,000229: 
016648,000230:                                                                                                  #  DSPCOUNT      ERASE                   # DISPLAY POSITION INDICATOR
016649,000231:                                                                                                  #  DECBRNCH      ERASE                   # +DEC, -DEC, OCT INDICATOR
016650,000232:                                                                                                  #  VERBREG       ERASE                   # VERB CODE
016651,000233:                                                                                                  #  NOUNREG       ERASE                   # NOUN CODE
016652,000234:                                                                                                  #  XREG          ERASE                   # R1 INPUT BUFFER
016653,000235:                                                                                                  #  YREG          ERASE                   # R2 INPUT BUFFER
016654,000236:                                                                                                  #  ZREG          ERASE                   # R3 INPUT BUFFER
016655,000237:                                                                                                  #  XREGLP        ERASE                   # LO PART OF XREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
016656,000238:                                                                                                  #  YREGLP        ERASE                   # LO PART OF YREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
016657,000239:                                                                                                  #  HITEMOUT      =       YREGLP          # TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS, MIN, SEC
016658,000240:                                                                                                  #                                        #       MUST = LOTEMOUT-1.
016659,000241:                                                                                                  #  ZREGLP        ERASE                   # LO PART OF ZREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
016660,000242:                                                                                                  #  LOTEMOUT      =       ZREGLP          # TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS, MIN, SEC
016661,000243:                                                                                                  #                                        #       MUST = HITEMOUT+1.
016662,000244:                                                                                                  #  MODREG        ERASE                   # MODE CODE
016663,000245:                                                                                                  #  DSPLOCK       ERASE                   # KEYBOARD/SUBROUTINE CALL INTERLOCK
016664,000246:                                                                                                  #  REQRET        ERASE                   # RETURN REGISTER FOR LOAD
016665,000247:                                                                                                  #  LOADSTAT      ERASE                   # STATUS INDICATOR FOR LOADTST
016666,000248:                                                                                                  #  CLPASS        ERASE                   # PASS INDICATOR FOR CLEAR
016667,000249:                                                                                                  #  NOUT          ERASE                   # ACTIVITY COUNTER FOR DSPTAB
016668,000250:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR      ERASE                   # MACHINE CADR FOR NOUN
016669,000251:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE       ERASE                   # N/V CODE FOR MONITOR. (= MONSAVE1-1)
016670,000252:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE1      ERASE                   # NOUNCADR FOR MONITOR (MATBS) = MONSAVE+1
016671,000253:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE2      ERASE                   # NVMONOPT OPTIONS
016672,000254:                                                                                                  #  DSPTAB        ERASE           +13D    # 0-10, DISPLAY PANEL BUFFER, 11-13, C RELAYS
016673,000255:                                                                                                  #  CADRSTOR      ERASE                   # ENDIDLE STORAGE
016674,000256:                                                                                                  #  NVQTEM        ERASE                   # NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING ADDRESS
016675,000257:                                                                                                  #                                        # MUST = NVBNKTEM-1.
016676,000258:                                                                                                  #  NVBNKTEM      ERASE                   # NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING BANK
016677,000259:                                                                                                  #                                        # MUST = NVQTEM+1
016678,000260:                                                                                                  #  VERBSAVE      ERASE                   # NEEDED FOR RECYCLE
016679,000261:                                                                                                  #  DSPLIST       ERASE                   # WAITING REG FOR DSP SYST INTERNAL USE
016680,000262:                                                                                                  #  EXTVBACT      ERASE                   # EXTENDED VERB ACTIVITY INTERLOCK
016681,000263:                                                                                                  #  DSPTEM1       ERASE                   # BUFFER STORAGE AREA 1 (MOSTLY FOR TIME)
016682,000264:                                                                                                  #  DSPTEM2       ERASE                   # BUFFER STORAGE AREA 2 (MOSTLY FOR DEG)
016683,000265: 
016684,000266:                                                                                                  #  END OF ERASABLES RESERVED FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION

016790,000372:                                                                                                  #  THE INPUT CODES ASSUMED FOR THE KEYBOARD ARE,
016791,000373:                                                                                                  #  0             10000
016792,000374:                                                                                                  #  1             00001
016793,000375:                                                                                                  #  9             01001
016794,000376:                                                                                                  #  VERB          10001
016795,000377:                                                                                                  #  ERROR RES     10010
016796,000378:                                                                                                  #  KEY RLSE      11001
016797,000379:                                                                                                  #  +             11010
016798,000380:                                                                                                  #  -             11011
016799,000381:                                                                                                  #  ENTER         11100
016800,000382:                                                                                                  #  CLEAR         11110
016801,000383:                                                                                                  #  NOUN          11111
016802,000384: 
016803,000385:                                                                                                  #  (2003 RSB -- The PROCEED key has no keycode; it is read by an alternate mechanism.)
016804,000386: 
016805,000387:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT FORMAT FOR DISPLAY PANEL.  SET OUT0 TO AAAABCCCCCDDDDD.
016806,000388:                                                                                                  #  A'S   SELECTS A RELAYWORD. THIS DETERMINES WHICH PAIR OF CHARACTERS ARE
016807,000389:                                                                                                  #        ENERGIZED.
016808,000390:                                                                                                  #  B     FOR SPECIAL RELAYS SUCH AS SIGNS ETC.
016809,000391:                                                                                                  #  C'S   5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR LEFT CHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD.
016810,000392:                                                                                                  #  D'S   5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR RIGHT CHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD.
016811,000393: 
016812,000394:                                                                                                  #  THE PANEL APPEARS AS FOLLOWS,
016813,000395:                                                                                                  #  MD1   MD2                             (MAJOR MODE)
016814,000396:                                                                                                  #  VD1   VD2 (VERB)      ND1     ND2     (NOUN)
016815,000397:                                                                                                  #  R1D1  R1D2    R1D3    R1D4    R1D5    (R1)
016816,000398:                                                                                                  #  R2D1  R2D2    R2D3    R2D4    R2D5    (R2)
016817,000399:                                                                                                  #  R3D1  R3D2    R3D3    R3D4    R3D5    (R3)
016818,000400: 
016819,000401:                                                                                                  #  EACH OF THESE IS GIVEN A DSPCOUNT NUMBER FOR USE WITHIN COMPUTATION ONLY
016820,000402: 
016821,000403:                                                                                                  #  MD1   25              R2D1    11              ALL ARE OCTAL
016822,000404:                                                                                                  #  MD2   24              R2D2    10
016823,000405:                                                                                                  #  VD1   23              R2D3     7
016824,000406:                                                                                                  #  VD2   22              R2D4     6
016825,000407:                                                                                                  #  ND1   21              R2D5     5
016826,000408:                                                                                                  #  ND2   20              R3D1     4
016827,000409:                                                                                                  #  R1D1  16              R3D2     3
016828,000410:                                                                                                  #  R1D2  15              R3D3     2
016829,000411:                                                                                                  #  R1D3  14              R3D4     1
016830,000412:                                                                                                  #  R1D4  13              R3D5     0
016831,000413:                                                                                                  #  R1D5  12
016832,000414: 
016833,000415:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS AN 11-REGISTER TABLE (DSPTAB) FOR THE DISPLAY PANEL.
016834,000416: 
016835,000417:                                                                                                  #  DSPTAB                RELAYWD         BIT11           BITS 10-6       BITS 5-1
016836,000418:                                                                                                  #  RELADD
016837,000419:                                                                                                  #  10            1011                            MD1 (25)        MD2 (24)
016838,000420:                                                                                                  #  9             1010                            VD1 (23)        VD2 (22)
016839,000421:                                                                                                  #  8             1001                            ND1 (21)        ND2 (20)
016840,000422:                                                                                                  #  7             1000                                            R1D1 (16)

Page 397 

016842,000424:                                                                                                  #  6             0111            +R1             R1D2 (15)       R1D3 (14)
016843,000425:                                                                                                  #  5             0110            -R1             R1D4 (13)       R1D5 (12)
016844,000426:                                                                                                  #  4             0101            +R2             R2D1 (11)       R2D2 (10)
016845,000427:                                                                                                  #  3             0100            -R2             R2D3 (7)        R2D4 (6)
016846,000428:                                                                                                  #  2             0011                            R2D5 (5)        R3D1 (4)
016847,000429:                                                                                                  #  1             0010            +R3             R3D2 (3)        R3D3 (2)
016848,000430:                                                                                                  #  0             0001            -R3             R3D4 (1)        R3D5 (0)
016849,000431:                                                                                                  #                0000        NO RELAYWORD
016850,000432: 
016851,000433:                                                                                                  #  THE 5-BIT OUTPUT RELAY CODES ARE:
016852,000434: 
016853,000435:                                                                                                  #  BLANK 00000
016854,000436:                                                                                                  #  0     10101
016855,000437:                                                                                                  #  1     00011
016856,000438:                                                                                                  #  2     11001
016857,000439:                                                                                                  #  3     11011
016858,000440:                                                                                                  #  4     01111
016859,000441:                                                                                                  #  5     11110
016860,000442:                                                                                                  #  6     11100
016861,000443:                                                                                                  #  7     10011
016862,000444:                                                                                                  #  8     11101
016863,000445:                                                                                                  #  9     11111
016864,000446: 
016865,000447:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT BITS USED BY PINBALL:
016866,000448: 
016867,000449:                                                                                                  #        KEY RELEASE LIGHT       -       BIT 5 OF CHANNEL 11
016868,000450:                                                                                                  #        VERB/NOUN FLASH         -       BIT 6 OF CHANNEL 11
016869,000451:                                                                                                  #        OPERATOR ERROR LIGHT    -       BIT 7 OF CHANNEL 11

Page 413 

017562,001144:                                                                                                  #  NOUN TABLES
017563,001145: 
017564,001146:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE L/40, NORMAL NOUN CASE.  NOUN CODE G/E 40, MIXED NOUN CASE.
017565,001147:                                                                                                  #  FOR NORMAL CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE       ECADR     FOR EACH NOUN.
017566,001148:                                                                                                  #  +0 INDICATES NOUN NOT USED.   - ENTRY INDICATES MACHINE CADR (E OR F) TO
017567,001149:                                                                                                  #  BE SPECIFIED. -1 INDICATES CHANNEL TO BE SPECIFIED.  -0 INDICATES AUGMENT
017568,001150:                                                                                                  #  OF LAST MACHINE CADR SUPPLIED.
017569,001151: 
017570,001152:                                                                                                  #  FOR MIXED CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE INDIRECT ADDRESS (IDADDREL) IN LOW
017571,001153:                                                                                                  #  10 BITS, AND THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER IN THE HIGH 5 BITS.
017572,001154: 
017573,001155:                                                                                                  #  NNTYPTAB IS A PACKED TABLE OF THE FORM MMMMMNNNNNPPPPP.
017574,001156: 
017575,001157:                                                                                                  #  FOR THE NORMAL CASE,  M'S ARE THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER.
017576,001158:                                                                                                  #                        N'S ARE THE SF ROUTINE CODE NUMBER.
017577,001159:                                                                                                  #                        P'S ARE THE SF CONSTANT CODE NUMBER.
017578,001160: 
017579,001161:                                                                                                  #  MIXED-CASE,           M'S ARE THE SF CONSTANT3 CODE NUMBER    3 COMPONENT CASE
017580,001162:                                                                                                  #                        N'S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER
017581,001163:                                                                                                  #                        P'S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
017582,001164:                                                                                                  #                        N'S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER    2 COMPONENT CASE
017583,001165:                                                                                                  #                        P'S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
017584,001166:                                                                                                  #                        P'S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER    1 COMPONENT CASE
017585,001167: 
017586,001168:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO AN INDIRECT ADDRESS TABLE (IDADDTAB) FOR MIXED CASE ONLY.
017587,001169:                                                                                                  #  EACH ENTRY CONTAINS ONE ECADR.    IDADDREL IS THE RELATIVE ADDRESS OF
017588,001170:                                                                                                  #  THE FIRST OF THESE ENTRIES.
017589,001171: 
017590,001172:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO A SCALE FACTOR ROUTINE NUMBER TABLE (RUTMXTAB) FOR MIXED
017591,001173:                                                                                                  #  CASE ONLY.  THERE IS ONE ENTRY PER MIXED NOUN.  THE FORM IS,
017592,001174: 
017593,001175:                                                                                                  #        QQQQQRRRRRSSSSS
017594,001176: 
017595,001177:                                                                                                  #  Q'S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 3 CODE NUMBER          3 COMPONENT CASE
017596,001178:                                                                                                  #  R'S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER
017597,001179:                                                                                                  #  S'S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
017598,001180:                                                                                                  #  R'S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER          2 COMPONENT CASE
017599,001181:                                                                                                  #  S'S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
017600,001182: 
017601,001183:                                                                                                  #  IN OCTAL DISPLAY AND LOAD (OCT OR DEC) VERBS, EXCLUDE USE OF VERBS WHOSE
017602,001184:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT NUMBER IS GREATER THAN THE NUMBER OF COMPONENTS IN NOUN.
017603,001185:                                                                                                  #  (ALL MACHINE ADDRESS TO BE SPECIFIED NOUNS ARE 3 COMPONENT.)
017604,001186: 
017605,001187:                                                                                                  #  IN MULTI-COMPONENT LOAD VERBS, NO MIXING OF OCTAL AND DECIMAL DATA
017606,001188:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT WORDS IS ALLOWED. ALARM IF VIOLATION.
017607,001189: 
017608,001190:                                                                                                  #  IN DECIMAL LOADS OF DATA, 5 NUMERICAL CHARACTERS MUST BE KEYED IN
017609,001191:                                                                                                  #  BEFORE EACH ENTER. IF NOT, ALARM.
017610,001192:

Page 414 

017612,001194:                                                                                                  #  DISPLAY VERBS
017613,001195: 
017614,001196: 41,2353           44752        DSPABC             CS       TWO                                   
017615,001197: 41,2354           02424                           TC       COMPTEST                              
017616,001198: 41,2355           50145                           INDEX    NOUNADD                               
017617,001199: 41,2356           40002                           CS       2                                     
017618,001200: 41,2357           56132                           XCH      BUF        +2                         
017619,001201: 41,2360           44753        DSPAB              CS       ONE                                   
017620,001202: 41,2361           02424                           TC       COMPTEST

018127,001709:                                                                                                  #  ANY NOUN, EXCEPT MIXED NOUNS. IT DISPLAYS THE CONTENTS
018128,001710:                                                                                                  #  OF THE REGISTER NOUNADD IS POINTING TO.  IF USED WITH NOUNS WHICH ARE
018129,001711:                                                                                                  #  INHERENTLY NOT DP SUCH AS THE CDU COUNTERS THE DISPLAY WILL BE GARBAGE.
018130,001712:                                                                                                  #  DISPLAY IS IN R1 AND R2 ONLY WITH THE SIGN IN R1.

Page 437 

018723,002305:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ALLOWS OTHER KEYBOARD ACTIVITY. IT IS ENDED BY VERB TERMINATE,
018724,002306:                                                                                                  #  VERB PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, VERB RESEQUENCE,
018725,002307:                                                                                                  #  ANOTHER MONITOR, OR ANY NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES THE DSPLOCK (PROVIDED
018726,002308:                                                                                                  #  THAT THE OPERATOR HAS SOMEHOW ALLOWED THE ENDING OF A MONITOR WHICH
018727,002309:                                                                                                  #  HE HAS INITIATED THROUGH THE KEYBOARD).
018728,002310: 
018729,002311:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ACTION IS SUSPENDED, BUT NOT ENDED, BY ANY KEYBOARD ACTION,
018730,002312:                                                                                                  #  EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET. IT BEGINS AGAIN WHEN KEY RELEASE IS PERFORMED.
018731,002313:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SAVES THE NOUN AND APPROPRIATE DISPLAY VERB IN MONSAVE. IT SAVES
018732,002314:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR IN MONSAVE1, IF NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED. BIT 15 OF
018733,002315:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE1 IS THE KILL MONITOR SIGNAL (KILLER BIT). BIT 14 OF MONSAVE1
018734,002316:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES THE CURRENT MONITOR WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED (EXTERNAL
018735,002317:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR BIT). IT IS TURNED OFF BY RELDSP AND KILMONON.
018736,002318: 
018737,002319:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE INDICATES IF MONITOR IS ON (+=ON, +0=OFF)
018738,002320:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +, MONITOR ENTERS NO REQUEST, BUT TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
018739,002321:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +0, MONITOR ENTERS REQUEST AND TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
018740,002322: 
018741,002323:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB (IF EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT IS OFF), VB=PROCEED WITHOUT DATA,
018742,002324:                                                                                                  #  VB=RESEQUENCE, AND VB=TERMINATE TURN KILL MONITOR BIT ON.
018743,002325: 
018744,002326:                                                                                                  #  IF KILLER BIT IS ON, MONREQ ENTERS NO FURTHER REQUESTS, ZEROS MONSAVE
018745,002327:                                                                                                  #  AND MONSAVE1 (TURNING OFF KILLER BIT AND EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT).
018746,002328: 
018747,002329:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR DOESNT TEST FOR MATBS SINCE NVSUB CAN HANDLE INTERNAL MATBS NOW.

018873,002455:                                                                                                  #  DSPFMEM IS USED TO DISPLAY (IN OCTAL) ANY FIXED REGISTER.
018874,002456:                                                                                                  #  IT IS USED WITH NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED. THE FCADR OF THE 
018875,002457:                                                                                                  #  DESIRED LOCATION IS THEN PUNCHED IN. IT HANDLES F/F (FCADR 4000-7777)
018876,002458:                                                                                                  #  
018877,002459:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27, THIS IS ENOUGH.
018878,002460: 
018879,002461:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30, THE THIRD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26 (PRIO, ADRES, BBCON)
018880,002462:                                                                                                  #  MUST BE PRELOADED WITH THE DESIRED SUPERBANK BITS (BITS 5,6,7).
018881,002463:                                                                                                  #        V23N26 SHOULD BE USED.
018882,002464: 
018883,002465:                                                                                                  #  SUMMARY
018884,002466:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27,                             V27N01E(FCADR)E
018885,002467:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30,     V23N26E(SUPERBITS)E     V27N01E(FCADR)E
018886,002468: 
018887,002469: 41,3353           34317        DSPFMEM            CAF      R1D1                                  #  IF F/F, DATACALL USES BANK 02 OR 03.
018888,002470: 41,3354           54777                           TS       DSPCOUNT                              
018889,002471: 41,3355           31047                           CA       DSPTEM1    +2                         #  SUPERBANK BITS WERE PRELOADED INTO
018890,002472: 41,3356           54001                           TS       L                                     #  3RD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26.
018891,002473: 41,3357           31017                           CA       NOUNCADR                              #  ORIGINAL FCADR LOADED STILL IN NOUNCADR.
018892,002474: 41,3360           04651                           TC       SUPDACAL                              #  CALL WITH FCADR IN A, SUPERBITS IN L.
018893,002475: 41,3361           03363                           TC       DSPOCTWO                              
018894,002476: 41,3362           05155        ENDSPF             TC       ENDOFJOB

019311,002893: 
019312,002894:                                                                                                  #  KEY RELEASE ROUTINE
019313,002895: 
019314,002896:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE ALWAYS TURNS OFF THE UPACT LIGHT AND ALWAYS CLEARS DSPLOCK.
019315,002897: 
019316,002898:                                                                                                  #  THE HIGHEST PRIORITY FUNCTION OF THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON IS THE
019317,002899:                                                                                                  #  UNSUSPENDING OF A SUSPENDED MONITOR WHICH WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED.
019318,002900:                                                                                                  #  THIS FUNCTION IS ACCOMPLISHED BY CLEARING DSPLOCK AND TURNING OFF
019319,002901:                                                                                                  #  THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IF BOTH DSPLIST AND CADRSTOR ARE EMPTY.
019320,002902: 
019321,002903:                                                                                                  #  IF NO SUCH MONITOR EXISTS, THEN RELDSP IS EXECUTED TO CLEAR DSPLOCK
019322,002904:                                                                                                  #  AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (FREEING THE DISPLAY SYSTEM FOR INTERNAL
019323,002905:                                                                                                  #  USE), TURN OFF THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT, AND WAKE UP ANY JOB IN DSPLIST.
019324,002906: 
019325,002907:                                                                                                  #  IN ADDITION IF THERE IS A JOB IN ENDIDLE, THEN CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED
019326,002908:                                                                                                  #  TO PINBRNCH (IN DISPLAY INTERFACE ROUTINE) TO RE-EXECUTE THE SERIES OF
019327,002909:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CALLS ETC. THAT PRECEDED THE ENDIDLE CALL STILL AWAITING RESPONSE.
019328,002910:                                                                                                  #  THIS FEATURE IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN THE OPERATOR HAS BEEN REQUESTED TO
019329,002911:                                                                                                  #  RESPOND TO SOME INTERNAL ACTION THAT USED ENDIDLE, BUT HE HAS WRITTEN
019330,002912:                                                                                                  #  OVER THE INFORMATION ON THE DISPLAY PANEL BY SOME DISPLAYS OF HIS OWN
019331,002913:                                                                                                  #  INITIATION WHICH DO NOT SERVE AS RESPONSES. HITTING KEYRLSE WILL
019332,002914:                                                                                                  #  RE-ESTABLISH THE DISPLAYS TO THE STATE THEY WERE IN BEOFRE HE OBSCURED
019333,002915:                                                                                                  #  THEM, SO THAT HE CAN SEE THE WAITING REQUEST. THIS WORKS ONLY FOR
019334,002916:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS THAT USED ENDIDLE THROUGH MARGARETS DISPLAY
019335,002917:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES.
019336,002918: 
019337,002919: 40,3461           44751        VBRELDSP           CS       BIT3                                  
019338,002920: 40,3462           00006                           EXTEND                                         
019339,002921: 40,3463           03011                           WAND     DSALMOUT                              #  TURN OFF UPACT LITE
019340,002922: 40,3464           10115                           CCS      21/22REG                              #  OLD DSPLOCK
019341,002923: 40,3465           34736                           CAF      BIT14                                 
019342,002924: 40,3466           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (EMB)
019343,002925: 40,3467           10000                           CCS      A                                     
019344,002926: 40,3470           03477                           TC       UNSUSPEN                              #  OLD DSPLOCK AND EMB BOTH 1, UNSUSPEND.
019345,002927: 40,3471           04457        TSTLTS4            TC       RELDSP                                #  NOT UNSUSPENDING EXTERNAL MONITOR,
019346,002928: 40,3472           11042                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #        RELEASE DISPLAY SYSTEM AND
019347,002929: 40,3473           03475                           TC       +2                                    #        DO RE-ESTABLISH IF CADRSTOR IS FULL.
019348,002930: 40,3474           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
019349,002931: 40,3475           04635                           TC       POSTJUMP                              
019350,002932: 40,3476           21050                           CADR     PINBRNCH                              
019351,002933: 40,3477           34755        UNSUSPEN           CAF      ZERO                                  #  EXTERNAL MONITOR IS SUSPENDED,
019352,002934: 40,3500           55012                           TS       DSPLOCK                               #        JUST UNSUSPEND IT BY CLEARING DSPLOCK.
019353,002935: 40,3501           11042                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #        TURN KEY RELEASE LIGHT OFF IF BOTH
019354,002936: 40,3502           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              #        CADRSTOR AND DSPLIST ARE EMPTY.
019355,002937: 40,3503           04502                           TC       RELDSP1                               
019356,002938: 40,3504           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
019357,002939: 
019358,002940: 40,3505                        ENDRELDS           EQUALS                                         
019359,002941:

Page 451 

019361,002943:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IS USED FOR SUBROUTINE CALLS FROM WITHIN COMPUTER. IT CAN BE
019362,002944:                                                                                                  #  USED TO CALL THE COMBINATION OF ANY DISPLAY, LOAD, OR MONITOR VERB
019363,002945:                                                                                                  #  TOGETHER WITH ANY NOUN AVAILABLE TO THE KEYBOARD.
019364,002946:                                                                                                  #  PLACE 0VVVVVVVNNNNNNN INTO A.
019365,002947:                                                                                                  #  V'S ARE THE 7-BIT VERB CODE.  N'S ARE THE 7-BIT NOUN CODE.
019366,002948: 
019367,002949:                                                                                                  #  IF NVSUB IS CALLED WTIH THE FOLLOWING NEGATIVE NUMBERS (RATHER THAN THE
019368,002950:                                                                                                  #  VERB-NOUN CODE) IN A, THEN THE DISPLAY IS BLANKED AS FOLLOWS -
019369,002951:                                                                                                  #   -4 FULL BLANK, -3 LEAVE MODE, -2 LEAVE MODE AND VERB, -1 BLANK R'S ONLY.
019370,002952: 
019371,002953:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CAN BE USED WTIH MACH CADR TO BE SPEC BY PLACING THE CADR INTO
019372,002954:                                                                                                  #  MPAC+2 BEFORE THE STANDARD NVSUB CALL.
019373,002955: 
019374,002956:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB RETURNS TO 2+ CALLING LOC AFTER PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
019375,002957:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS AVAIALBLE. THE NEW NOUN AND VERB CODES ARE DISPLAYED.
019376,002958:                                                                                                  #  IF V'S =0, THE NEW NOUN CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY (RETURN WITH NO FURTHER
019377,002959:                                                                                                  #  ACTION). IF N'S =0, THE NEW VERB CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY (RETURN WITH NO
019378,002960:                                                                                                  #  FURTHER ACTION).
019379,002961: 
019380,002962:                                                                                                  #  IT RETURNS TO 1+ CALLING LOC WITHOUT PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
019381,002963:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS BLOCKED (NOTHING IS DISPLAYED IN THIS CASE).
019382,002964:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES TC ABORT (WITH OCT 01501) IF IT ENCOUNTERS A DISPLAY PROGRAM
019383,002965:                                                                                                  #  ALARM CONDITION BEFORE RETURN TO CALLER.
019384,002966: 
019385,002967:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS BLOCKED BY THE DEPRESSION OF ANY
019386,002968:                                                                                                  #  KEY, EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET.
019387,002969:                                                                                                  #  IT IS RELEASED BY THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON, ALL EXTENDED VERBS,
019388,002970:                                                                                                  #  PROCED WITHOUT DATA, TERMINATE, RESEQUENCE, INITIALIZE EXECUTIVE,
019389,002971:                                                                                                  #  RECALL PART OF RECALTST IF ENDIDLE WAS USED,
019390,002972:                                                                                                  #  VB = REQUEST EXECUTIVE, VB = REQUEST WAITLIST,
019391,002973:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SET UP.
019392,002974: 
019393,002975:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS ALSO BLOCKED BY THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT, WHICH
019394,002976:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES AND EXTERNALLY INITIATED MONITOR IS RUNNING (SEE MONITOR).
019395,002977: 
019396,002978:                                                                                                  #  A NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES DSPLOCK AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT ENDS OLD
019397,002979:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR.
019398,002980: 
019399,002981:                                                                                                  #  DSPLOCK IS THE INTERLOCK FOR USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM WHICH
019400,002982:                                                                                                  #  LOCKS OUT INTERNAL USE WHENEVER THERE IS EXTERNAL KEYBOARD ACTION.
019401,002983: 
019402,002984:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB SHOULD BE USED TWICE IN SUCCESSION FOR 'PLEASE PERFORM' SITUATIONS
019403,002985:                                                                                                  #  (SIMILARLY FOR PLEASE MARK).  FIRST PLACE THE CODED NUMBER FOR WHAT
019404,002986:                                                                                                  #  ACTION IS DESIRED OF OPERATOR INTO THE REGISTERS REFERRED TO BY THE
019405,002987:                                                                                                  #  'CHECKLIST' NOUN. GO TO NVSUB WITH A DISPLAY VERB AND THE 'CHECKLIST'
019406,002988:                                                                                                  #  NOUN.  GO TO NVSUB AGAIN WTIH THE 'PLEASE PERFORM' VERB AND ZEROS IN THE
019407,002989:                                                                                                  #  LOW 7 BITS. THIS 'PASTES UP' THE 'PLEASE PERFORM' VERB INTO THE VERB
019408,002990:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS.
019409,002991: 
019410,002992:                                                                                                  #  NVMONOPT IS AN ENTRY SIMILAR TO NVSUB, BUT REQUIRING AN ADDITIONAL

Page 452 

019412,002994:                                                                                                  #  PARAMETER IN L. IT SHOULD BE USED ONLY WITH A MONITOR VERB-NOUN CODE IN
019413,002995:                                                                                                  #  A. AFTER EACH MONITOR DISPLAY A *PLEASE* VERB WILL BE PASED INT THE VERB
019414,002996:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS OR DATA WILL BE BLANKED (OR BOTH) ACCORDING TO THE OPTIONS
019415,002997:                                                                                                  #  SPECIFIED IN L. IF BITS 8-14 OF L ARE OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL 
019416,002998:                                                                                                  #  BE INTERPRETED AS A VERB CODE AND PASTED IN THE VERB LIGHTS. (THIS VERB
019417,002999:                                                                                                  #  CODE SHOULD DESIGNATE ONE OF THE *PLEASE* VERBS.)  IF BITS 1-3 OF L ARE
019418,003000:                                                                                                  #  OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL BE USED TO BLANK DATA BY BEING FED TO
019419,003001:                                                                                                  #  BLANKSUB.  IF NVMONOPT IS USED WITH A VERB OTHER THAN A MONITOR VERB,
019420,003002:                                                                                                  #  THE PARAMETER IN L HAS NO EFFECT.
019421,003003: 
019422,003004:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IN FIXED-FIXED PLACES 2+CALLING LOC INTO NVQTEM, TC NVSUBEND INTO
019423,003005:                                                                                                  #  ENTRET. (THIS WILL RESTORE OLD CALLING BANK BITS)
019424,003006: 
019425,003007:    4154                                           SETLOC   ENDALM     +1                         
019426,003008: 
019427,003009:    4154                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN

019429,003011:    4155           54123        NVMONOPT           TS       NVTEMP

019532,003114:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR IN ENTPAS0 (INTMCTBS).
019533,003115: 
019534,003116:    4204                                           SETLOC   NVSUBEND   +2                         
019535,003117:    4204                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
019536,003118:                                                                                                  #  FORCE BIT 15 OF MONSAVE1 TO 1.
019537,003119:    4204           34735        KILMONON           CAF      BIT15                                 #        THIS IS THE KILL MONITOR BIT.
019538,003120:    4205           55021                           TS       MONSAVE1                              #  TURN OFF BIT 14, THE EXTERNAL
019539,003121:                                                                                                  #        MONITOR BIT.
019540,003122:    4206           00002                           TC       Q                                     
019541,003123: 
019542,003124:                                                                                                  #  LOADSTAT      +0      INACTIVE (WAITING FOR DATA). SET BY NVSUB
019543,003125:                                                                                                  #                +1      PROCEED NO DATA. SET BY SPECIAL VERB
019544,003126:                                                                                                  #                -1      TERMINATE. SET BY SPECIAL VERB.
019545,003127:                                                                                                  #                -0              DATA IN         SET BY END OF LOAD ROUTINE
019546,003128:                                                                                                  #                        OR      RESEQUENCE      SET BY VERB 32
019547,003129: 
019548,003130:                                                                                                  #  L TO ENDIDLE (FIXED FIXED)
019549,003131:                                                                                                  #  ROUTINES THAT REQUEST LOADS THROUGH NVSUB SHOULD USE ENDIDLE WHILE
019550,003132:                                                                                                  #  WAITING FOR THE DATA TO BE LOADED. ENDIDLE PUTS CURRENT JOB TO SLEEP.
019551,003133:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
019552,003134:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOB SLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
019553,003135:                                                                                                  #  RECALTST TESTS LOADSTAT AND WAKES JOB UP TO,
019554,003136:                                                                                                  #        L+1     FOR TERMINATE
019555,003137:                                                                                                  #        L+2     FOR PROCEED WITHOUT DATA
019556,003138:                                                                                                  #        L+3     FOR DATA IN, OR RESEQUENCE
019557,003139:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES NOTHING IF LOADSTAT INDICATES WAITING FOR DTA.
019558,003140: 
019559,003141:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE ABORTS (WITH CODE 1206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO SLEEP

Page 455 

019561,003143:                                                                                                  #  IN PINBALL. IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO ENDIDLE WHEN
019562,003144:                                                                                                  #  1)    CADRSTOR NOT= +0. THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF ENDIDLE IS
019563,003145:                                                                                                  #        EXCEEDED. (+-NZ INDICATES A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDDLE.)
019564,003146:                                                                                                  #  2)    DSPLIST NOT= +0. THIS INDICATES A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO
019565,003147:                                                                                                  #        NVSUBUSY.
019566,003148: 
019567,003149:    4207           22002        ENDIDLE            LXCH     Q                                     #  RETURN ADDRESS INTO L.
019568,003150:    4210           04220                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0
019569,003151:    4211           04224                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0
019570,003152:    4212           30001                           CA       L                                     #  DONT SET DSPLOC TO 1 SO CAN USE
019571,003153:    4213           75012                           MASK     LOW10                                 #  ENDIDLE WITH NVSUB INITIATED MONITOR.
019572,003154:    4214           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  SAME STRATEGY FOR CADR AS MAKECADR.
019573,003155:    4215           55042                           TS       CADRSTOR                              
019574,003156:    4216           05133                           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
019575,003157: 
019576,003158:    4217           05155        ENDINST            TC       ENDOFJOB                              
019577,003159: 
019578,003160:    4220           11042        ISCADR+0           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #  ABORTS (CODE 01206) IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
019579,003161:    4221           04227                           TC       DSPABORT                              #  RETURNS IF CADRSTOR = +0.
019580,003162:    4222           00002                           TC       Q                                     
019581,003163:    4223           04227                           TC       DSPABORT

019584,003166:    4225           04227                           TC       DSPABORT                              #  RETURNS IF DSPLIST = +0.

019620,003202:                                                                                                  #  BLANKSUB BLANKS ANY COMBINATION OF R1, R2, R3.
019621,003203:                                                                                                  #  CALL WITH BLANKING CODE IN A.
